mkdir -p build-TEENSY41/genhdr
Create build-TEENSY41/genhdr/pins.h
python3 boards/make-pins.py --board boards/TEENSY41/pins.csv --af boards/MIMXRT1062_af.csv\
		--iomux /Users/georgerosar/Documents/GitHub/iridescentCoconutSynth/micropython/lib/nxp_driver/sdk/devices/MIMXRT1062/drivers/fsl_iomuxc.h \
		--prefix boards/mimxrt_prefix.c --hdr build-TEENSY41/genhdr/pins.h > build-TEENSY41/pins_gen.c

python3 boards/make-flexram-config.py -d ../../lib/nxp_driver/sdk/devices/MIMXRT1062/MIMXRT1062.h \
		-f ../../lib/nxp_driver/sdk/devices/MIMXRT1062/MIMXRT1062_features.h -l boards/MIMXRT1062.ld -c MIMXRT1062 > build-TEENSY41/flexram_config.s
